Grains: The Downriver Rice Market Is Explicitly Stable and Implicitly Firm

South City: The arrival of goods from various merchant groups is lacking due to wind resistance, and the accumulation of water in the rivers is dwindling, resulting in a bleak atmosphere throughout the city. Transactions are sporadic. There is not much supply of indica rice from various places, and the inventory in Shanghai is low. In addition, there was a hurricane, and ships obstructed on the route are difficult to reach the port. If prices increase, the Social Affairs Bureau will send personnel to supervise the market and strictly prohibit further increases. They will also investigate the inventory, so the prices of goods can only temporarily remain at their original levels.

New Gate: The supply of Qingjiao (green glutinous rice), Suzhou, Changzhou, and other sources in the west road is still scarce. The sales of 洋蘆尖 (Yánglújiān, foreign pointed rice) are active among customer merchants, and the rice sales are also good. Prices have increased by 0.1 chi (approximately 1.1 inches). The price of thin indica and thick japonica rice has been set within a limited range since the market opened, and it is explicitly stable but implicitly firm. The assessment prices have not been officially published, but it is rumored that there are about 30 to 40 ships obstructed on the route. Foreign rice customer merchants and local sales seem to be slightly quiet.

The Flour Market Suddenly Plummets

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, the prices of each month suddenly plummeted. There are two main reasons for the plunge. One is the surplus of American wheat, which is seen in detailed international telegrams. It is a matter of course that it will be dumped in China in the future. Second, domestic factories and small and medium-sized factories in Shanghai intend to purchase a large amount of American wheat, amounting to 200,000 tons. This news has spread widely among the inland merchant groups. This alarming rumor has frightened many inland bulls who are purely speculative. The volume of sales by factories reached 600,000 to 700,000 bags throughout the day. Therefore, the sharp rise of a few days ago was frustrated, and prices plummeted step by step. Looking ahead, if the trend of foreign wheat is not good, domestic disasters and natural disasters will inevitably be dominated by foreign forces. As a result, this month fell by 0.35, September fell by 0.425, October fell by 0.475, November fell by 0.45, December fell by 0.525, and January fell by 0.4.

Wheat Prices Fall Consistently and Sharply

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning and afternoon, the prices of each month presented a state of sharp decline. With the alarming news of a surplus overseas, the purchase of foreign wheat seems to be no problem. In addition, large bulls gradually released their positions, and speculators seemed to have lost their central force. Therefore, the selling pressure in each month was extremely strong, and prices fell sharply step by step in each session. The next step is to look at the foreign wheat report and then determine the future trend. As a result, this month and September plummeted by 0.1 qian compared to the previous day, October fell by 0.09 qian, November fell by 0.1 qian, and December fell by 0.09 qian. The spot wheat market is still stable due to low inventory and active factory demand. 7,400 bags of Nanjing, Hezhou, Zhenjiang, Danyang, Penglai, Taicang, Shuangfeng, Weiting, Sijing, Zhintang, and other wheat were opened. Fuxin bought 1,700 bags, Shenda bought 2,400 bags, and Huafeng bought 3,500 bags.

Sugar Market: Dutch Red Sugar Opens Exceptionally Well

Yesterday, a telegram from the sugar market production area stated that the price of Cuban spot sugar had not changed from the previous telegram. New York sugar futures for September and December also lacked fluctuations. Prices for March and May of the next year each fell by 0.01. Java spot and futures sugar remained unchanged. At the association market, white sugar made from Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse sand was very quiet in buying. Ordinary goods were 11.45 taels, and slightly higher goods were 11.55 taels. White sugar made from No. 20 medium sand was 11 taels. Transactions were scarce. The market was still firm. 太古 (Taikoo) B was 11.1 taels, DY was 11.95 taels, and demand was sluggish. HX was 11.85 taels, HM was 11.4 to 11.45 taels, and the trend was firm. More than 300 bags of O25 were opened at a price of 9.35 yuan. The market was also not weak. In the number盤, Bingchang sold more than 1,000 bags of No. 9 Dutch red sugar at a price of 9.45 yuan. The dealer's intention to buy was quite strong, and the market was exceptionally strong.

Dried Goods: The Screening Process of Guizhou Longan May Increase Again

Longan is rare because the arrival volume is scarce, and the number of盤s is gradually increasing. In addition, the inventory has all been baked, and the cost has increased significantly. If it is still sold at the original price, it will inevitably result in losses. Based on the recent offer prices, the top-quality product has a cost of nearly 40 taels after further selection. Therefore, the industry association decided yesterday to increase the price of screened Guizhou longan across the board to maintain capital. The prices are as follows: top-quality sells for 38 taels, supreme-quality sells for 28 taels, super-quality sells for 22 taels, and split-open sells for 15 taels.

Orchid Seeds Fall by One Tael

Since the new orchid seeds came out, the number arriving has not been large because they are not yet the 正水 (zhèngshuǐ, peak season) goods. Therefore, the collection is limited. Yesterday, another ten or so boxes arrived on the Jinan round, and they have already been opened. The price has decreased by one tael compared to the previous盤. It is said that the 正水 goods may also enter the market in ten days. According to Hankou reports, this year's harvest is still abundant. If they pour in later, the market price may loosen.

Silk and Tea: Yuhang Autumn Silkworm Seed Preparation is Relatively Smooth

Farmers in the Yuhang area, because the spring and summer silkworm crops this year were generally unsuccessful, are preparing to raise autumn silkworms to make up for the losses. They have ordered a large number of improved seed papers from the Provincial Sericulture Field and various seed production fields and have now paid for them separately. Farmers are now starting to select seeds in preparation for hatching.

European Sales of Zhenmei Green Tea Continue to be Strong

Yesterday, banks like Luzhuang Tuzhuang were involved in Zhenmei green tea, with companies such as Xiehe Yihé Tongfu Yongxing showing strong interest. The prices of goods from Wudong Tunxi and other regions have already increased to 120-130 taels. The market is extremely firm. For Gongxi items, the Russian Assistance Association is very interested. Baitouzhuang and China Tea Company also have demand. The trend in the tea market is increasingly optimistic.

Silk Sales in Europe and America Still Show No Improvement

Yesterday, the silk market of foreign banks in Shanghai still showed no improvement. It was found that silk sales in the European and American markets were not improving, and telegrams were silent. The market atmosphere was stagnant. Only Zhonghe bought 15 bales of white dried silk, and Xinfu bought 20 bales of gray dried silk. Prices remained firm.

Social News

Major Merger in American Petroleum Company

Impact Will Spread Worldwide

New York News: Mergers among major American petroleum companies are frequent. Recently, following the merger of New York Standard Oil and Vacuum Oil to form Socony-Vacuum Corporation, New Jersey Standard Oil and California Standard Oil are also discussing a merger. After establishment, the aforementioned newly merged Socony-Vacuum Corporation will further merge, realizing a large petroleum trust encompassing most of the Standard Oil system. The daily production capacity of each company owned by Socony-Vacuum Corporation is as follows (unit: barrels):

Refining Capacity Production Capacity

New York Standard Oil 34,000 16,000

Magnolia 96,000 62,500

Chalmette 99,000

White Eagle 14,500 12,000

Vacuum 26,500 12,000

Other 20,600 15,000

Total 290,700 118,000

The combined capital after the merger will reach US$100 million. On the other hand, New Jersey's authorized capital is US$75 million (paid-in US$63,609,175, previous year's surplus US$12,090,279.94), California's authorized capital is 15 million shares without par value (paid-in 13,016,434 shares, previous year's surplus US$46,633,490). The implementation of the merger of these three companies constitutes a massive petroleum corporation, and its impact will spread worldwide.

Social News Submission Guidelines

(1) Text limited to news concerning domestic and international science, industry, commerce, agriculture.

(2) News concerning hygiene, aviation, exploration, customs, or urban life. Pictures limited to various lyrical paintings concerning social life.

(3) Photographs of seasonal events, scenery, flora and fauna, figures, and news photography are acceptable. Photographs of beautiful women in scenic landscapes are especially welcome.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(6) Do not write in vertical columns. Avoid cursive script. Western text should be minimized. If necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

(7) Do not use ink for drawings. Do not use colored paper. Black drawings on white paper are required.

(8) Please specify "Social News Editorial Department" as the recipient for submissions.

Shanghai Market

Market News

Sanyou Industrial Society on Nanjing Road announces that the company has specially established a Bargain Sale Department starting yesterday. Dozens of items such as towels, clothing, children's wear, bed sheets, bathrobes, socks, etc., will be greatly discounted. The opportunity is extremely rare, etc.

Theater News

Changming Film Company announces that its new six-part film, Pingyang City, was filmed on location at Mount Tai, capturing many historical sites and famous scenic spots. Watching this film in this hot summer is like escaping the heat in person, feeling the depths of the mountains, the greenness of the water, and a sense of coolness. This episode is the conclusion of the entire Pingyang City series. All the essences and key moments are explained together in this episode. Those who love watching Pingyang City films should not miss this last chance to see Qiubo's performance, etc.

Medical News

National physician Gu Weichuan has retired to a two-story western-style house at No. 18, Bing, along Baker Road. Although he no longer practices, many patients with febrile diseases still seek his diagnosis. His son, Hongzhang, continues to practice at the original location in the Beixing Lane, North Nicheng Bridge. For several months, patients have been coming in droves, saving countless lives. Prominent figures in Shanghai, such as Historian Shen Qiquan, wrote inscriptions on prescriptions; Zhang Yanchang, Chuanshi, presented a plaque inscription written by Liu Runqin, Dianzhuan; Li Fusun presented an inscription written by Jiang Guodong, Taishi; yesterday, lawyer Tao Jiachun also presented lawyer Wu Zhiping with a golden plaque, which was delivered with a colorful pavilion and military band, attracting a large crowd of onlookers, all admiring Gu Jun's ability to carry on his father's legacy.

Shanghai New Hospital, across from the Central Grand Theater on Six Malu, announces that since hiring Dr. Zhong Dingshen, a famous physician who previously served as a military doctor, business has been very prosperous, as Dr. Zhong's surgery is highly skilled and has the effect of curing illnesses with medicine, etc.

Traditional Chinese medicine practitioner Wu Keqian announces that his residence is at No. 23, Weihou Lane, Lafayette Road (east of Beiler Road). He previously ran the Medical News newspaper and enjoyed a high reputation at the time. In recent years, he has focused on consultations and has unique insights into various fields such as measles, epidemic diseases, typhoid fever, and malaria. He has saved many people's lives. Recently, a child from the Zheng family on Beiler Road suffered from severe asthma due to measles and was on the verge of death. Also, Mr. Wu from Yuanyuan Lane, Tiantong'an Road, Zhabei, suffered from high fever and delirium for several days. Both were saved and cured by this doctor, and both families are very grateful, etc.
